{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01LuStWjsKPb7y95z7YHJmGg","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01WTYkW8XvAqNxLKs58g9zpB","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/RELEASE_NOTES.md","content":"# Flipt Release Notes\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\n> These changes require action from users upgrading.\n\n### API Evaluation Endpoints - Migrating from Legacy Evaluate Methods\n\nThe legacy `Flipt.Evaluate` and `Flipt.BatchEvaluate` RPC methods are **deprecated** and will be removed in a future release.\n\n**Migration Path:**\n- **For Boolean Flags**: Use the dedicated `EvaluationService.Boolean(EvaluationRequest)` endpoint instead\n- **For Variant Flags**: Use the dedicated `EvaluationService.Variant(EvaluationRequest)` endpoint instead\n- **For Batch Operations**: Use `EvaluationService.Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest)` for batched evaluations\n\nThe new evaluation API provides structured response types (`BooleanEvaluationResponse`, `VariantEvaluationResponse`, and `ErrorEvaluationResponse`) that offer better type safety and clearer semantics compared to the legacy single-response structure.\n\n**Example:**\n```protobuf\n// Old API (deprecated)\nrpc Evaluate(EvaluationRequest) returns (EvaluationResponse)\n\n// New API\nrpc Boolean(EvaluationRequest) returns (BooleanEvaluationResponse)\nrpc Variant(EvaluationRequest) returns (VariantEvaluationResponse)\n```\n\n### Pagination API Change - Offset to Cursor-Based Pagination\n\nThe `offset` parameter is **deprecated** in list request messages:\n- `ListNamespaceRequest`\n- `ListFlagRequest`\n- `ListSegmentRequest`\n- `ListRuleRequest`\n\n**Migration Path:**\nReplace all `offset`-based pagination with the `page_token` parameter:\n- Use `page_token` returned in the `next_page_token` field of list responses for pagination\n- Remove reliance on `offset` parameter\n- If you need to restart pagination, don't provide `page_token` (equivalent to offset=0)\n\n**Example:**\n```protobuf\n// Before (deprecated)\nmessage ListFlagRequest {\n  int32 limit = 1;\n  int32 offset = 2;  // [deprecated]\n}\n\n// After\nmessage ListFlagRequest {\n  int32 limit = 1;\n  int32 offset = 2;     // [deprecated = true]\n  string page_token = 3; // Use this instead\n}\n```\n\n### Single Segment to Multi-Segment Rules\n\nThe `segment_key` field is **deprecated** in favor of the new `segment_keys` array and `segment_operator` field for rules and rollouts.\n\n**Migration Path:**\n- Rules: Update to use `segment_keys` (array) and `segment_operator` (OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR or AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR) instead of single `segment_key`\n- Rollouts: Update to use `RolloutSegment.segment_keys` and `segment_operator` instead of `segment_key`\n- The old fields will continue to work but may be removed in a future release\n\n**Example:**\n```protobuf\n// Before (deprecated)\nmessage CreateRuleRequest {\n  string flag_key = 1;\n  string segment_key = 2;  // [deprecated = true]\n}\n\n// After - Support multiple segments with operators\nmessage CreateRuleRequest {\n  string flag_key = 1;\n  string segment_key = 2;              // [deprecated = true]\n  repeated string segment_keys = 5;    // Use this\n  SegmentOperator segment_operator = 6; // AND or OR\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### Enhanced Evaluation API with Type-Specific Endpoints\n\n**Component: gRPC Evaluation Service (`flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService`)**\n\nNew dedicated evaluation endpoints for better API clarity and type safety:\n- `Boolean(EvaluationRequest)` → `BooleanEvaluationResponse` - For boolean flag evaluation\n- `Variant(EvaluationRequest)` → `VariantEvaluationResponse` - For variant flag evaluation\n- `Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest)` → `BatchEvaluationResponse` - For batched evaluations\n\nResponse types now distinguish between success and error cases with `EvaluationResponseType` enum (VARIANT_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE, BOOLEAN_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE, ERROR_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE).\n\n### Multiple Segment Support in Rules and Rollouts\n\n**Component: Rules and Rollouts API**\n\nRules and rollouts can now reference multiple segments with AND/OR logic:\n- `SegmentOperator` enum: OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR (default) or AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR\n- Rules support `repeated string segment_keys` with `SegmentOperator`\n- Rollouts support `RolloutSegment.segment_keys` with `segment_operator`\n\nThis enables complex targeting scenarios such as:\n- Rule matches if entity is in \"beta_users\" AND \"premium_subscribers\"\n- Rollout targets all users EXCEPT those matching specific segments\n\n### Boolean Flag Type and Evaluation\n\n**Component: Core Flags API**\n\nNew FlagType enum value: `BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE` (in addition to existing VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE)\n\nBoolean flags have dedicated evaluation endpoints:\n- `EvaluationService.Boolean()` - Returns `BooleanEvaluationResponse` with enabled/disabled state\n- Boolean rollouts: `RolloutThreshold` type supports percentage-based rollouts with boolean values\n- Boolean rules: Can distribute boolean true/false values through distributions\n\n**API Example:**\n```protobuf\nmessage CreateFlagRequest {\n  string key = 1;\n  string name = 2;\n  FlagType type = 6; // VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE or BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE\n}\n```\n\n### Advanced Constraint Operators\n\n**Component: Constraints API**\n\nNew constraint operators for segment targeting:\n- `IS ONE OF` - Value matches one of the provided values\n- `IS NOT ONE OF` - Value does not match any of the provided values\n\nThese work with existing comparison types: STRING_COMPARISON_TYPE, NUMBER_COMPARISON_TYPE, BOOLEAN_COMPARISON_TYPE, DATETIME_COMPARISON_TYPE, ENTITY_ID_COMPARISON_TYPE.\n\n### Entity ID Constraint Type\n\n**Component: Constraints API**\n\nNew `ENTITY_ID_COMPARISON_TYPE` for constraint evaluation enables comparing entity IDs directly in segment constraints, useful for allow-listing or block-listing specific users/entities.\n\n### Namespaced Authentication Tokens\n\n**Component: Auth API (`flipt.auth.AuthenticationMethodTokenService`)**\n\nAuthentication tokens can now be scoped to specific namespaces:\n- `CreateTokenRequest` includes optional `namespace_key` field\n- Namespaced tokens can only access resources within their designated namespace\n- Improves multi-tenant security and isolation\n\n**API Example:**\n```protobuf\nmessage CreateTokenRequest {\n  string name = 1;\n  string description = 2;\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp expires_at = 3;\n  string namespace_key = 4; // Optional: scope to namespace\n}\n```\n\n### GitHub Authentication with Team Membership\n\n**Component: Auth API (`flipt.auth.AuthenticationMethodGithubService`)**\n\nGitHub authentication now supports team membership verification:\n- Check if authenticated user belongs to specific GitHub organization teams\n- Adds `AuthenticationMethodGithubService` with OAuth flow support\n- Complements existing GitHub organization membership checks\n\n### JWT Authentication Method\n\n**Component: Auth API**\n\nNew JWT authentication method available:\n- `Method.METHOD_JWT` enum value\n- Enables JWT token validation for API authentication\n- Supports custom JWT claims and validation rules\n\n### Multi-Storage Backend Support\n\n**Component: Storage Layer**\n\nEnhanced support for multiple storage backends:\n- **S3 Filesystem Backend**: S3 bucket support with prefix filtering for organized data structures\n- **Google Cloud Storage (GCS)**: Full GCS integration for filesystem-based flag storage\n- **Azure Blob Storage**: Azure integration for filesystem operations\n- **OCI (Object Container Interface)**: OCI storage with AWS ECR integration and configurable manifest versions\n- **LibSQL/Turso**: SQLite-compatible database support\n\nEach backend integrates with the filesystem abstraction layer supporting both SQL and non-SQL deployments.\n\n### Directory Scope for Git Backend\n\n**Component: Storage/Git Backend (`fs/git`)**\n\nNew configuration support for Git-based flag storage:\n- `directory_scope` parameter for limiting Git operations to a specific directory\n- Useful for monorepos or multi-service Git repositories\n- Restricts flag definitions to a designated directory subtree\n\n### Working Directory Support for Flipt Validate\n\n**Component: CLI (flipt validate)**\n\n`flipt validate` command now accepts a working directory parameter:\n- Allows validation to run in a specific directory context\n- Useful in CI/CD pipelines with multiple flag definitions\n- Validates flag YAML/CUE schemas in the specified directory\n\n### Rollout Descriptions\n\n**Component: Rollouts API**\n\nRollouts can now include descriptions:\n- `Rollout.description` field for documenting rollout purpose and logic\n- Included in rollout cards in the UI\n- Helps teams understand complex rollout strategies\n\n### Analytics with Clickhouse Support\n\n**Component: Analytics API (`flipt.analytics.AnalyticsService`)**\n\nNew analytics backend and API:\n- `AnalyticsService.GetFlagEvaluationsCount()` - Retrieves evaluation count metrics\n- Clickhouse database integration for time-series analytics\n- Supports time range queries (from/to parameters)\n- Returns timestamps and evaluation values for visualization\n\n**API Example:**\n```protobuf\nrpc GetFlagEvaluationsCount(GetFlagEvaluationsCountRequest)\n    returns (GetFlagEvaluationsCountResponse)\n\nmessage GetFlagEvaluationsCountRequest {\n  string namespace_key = 1;\n  string flag_key = 2;\n  string from = 3;  // Timestamp\n  string to = 4;    // Timestamp\n}\n```\n\n### Kubernetes Authentication Provider (SDK)\n\n**Component: SDK/Go Auth**\n\nNew Kubernetes service account authentication provider for SDK:\n- `AuthenticationMethodKubernetesService.VerifyServiceAccount()`\n- Enables pod-to-pod authentication using Kubernetes service account tokens\n- Useful for Kubernetes-native deployments\n\n### Redis Cache Improvements\n\n**Component: Storage/Cache**\n\nEnhanced Redis cache configuration:\n- Support for Redis username in authentication (in addition to password)\n- Improved connection handling\n- Only stores authentication hashes in cache (not full credentials)\n\n---\n\n## Deprecations\n\n### Legacy Evaluate RPC Methods\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.40.0 (or earlier)\n- **What**: `Flipt.Evaluate()` and `Flipt.BatchEvaluate()` RPC methods\n- **Replacement**: Use `EvaluationService.Boolean()`, `EvaluationService.Variant()`, or `EvaluationService.Batch()`\n- **Timeline**: Will be removed in a future major version\n\n### Offset-Based Pagination\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.13.0\n- **What**: `offset` field in list requests (ListFlagRequest, ListSegmentRequest, ListRuleRequest, ListNamespaceRequest)\n- **Replacement**: Use `page_token` for cursor-based pagination\n- **Timeline**: ~1 year from deprecation date (June 2024)\n\n### Single Segment Fields\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.31.0+\n- **What**: `segment_key` field in `CreateRuleRequest`, `UpdateRuleRequest`, `RolloutSegment.segment_key`\n- **Replacement**: Use `segment_keys` (array) with `segment_operator` for AND/OR logic\n- **Timeline**: ~1 year from deprecation date\n\n### Jaeger Tracing Exporter\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.36.0\n- **What**: Jaeger tracing exporter support\n- **Replacement**: Use OpenTelemetry Protocol (OTLP) with official Jaeger OTLP receiver\n- **Reason**: OpenTelemetry dropped official Jaeger exporter support in July 2023\n- **Timeline**: Already removed in recent versions\n\n### Authentication Metadata Exclusion Configuration\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.37.0\n- **What**: `authentication.exclude.metadata` configuration option\n- **Replacement**: Configure metadata handling directly in auth method settings\n- **Timeline**: ~6 months from deprecation date (May 2024)\n\n---\n\n## Bug Fixes\n\n### Critical Fixes\n\n- **isnotoneof Operator Logic**: Fixed operator using incorrect logic for segment constraint evaluation (#2912)\n- **Segment Constraints in Different Namespaces**: Resolved issue where segment constraints with the same key in different namespaces caused evaluation errors (#2920)\n- **Batch Evaluation exclude_not_found**: Fixed batched evaluation to properly exclude not-found responses when requested\n\n### Authentication & Security\n\n- **Auth Cache Security**: Only store authentication hash in cache, not full credentials (#2974)\n- **Database Connection Optimization**: Skip establishing database connection in auth when unnecessary (#2973)\n- **Email Matching on OIDC**: Only enforce email matches on OIDC method tokens, not other auth methods (#1934)\n\n### Configuration & Validation\n\n- **Trace Log Level Schema**: Fixed invalid trace log level schema validation\n- **Rollout Segment JSON Schema**: Corrected jsonschema validation for key|keys in rollout segment definitions (#2947)\n- **Page Token Validation**: Return 400 for invalid page token instead of internal error\n\n### UI/Console Fixes\n\n- **Evaluation Console Context Warning**: Fixed UI to properly show warnings about context values in evaluation console (#2937)\n- **Uppercase Letters in Keys**: Fixed UI removing uppercase letters from flag/segment keys (#2790)\n- **Boolean Constraint Type**: Fixed boolean constraint type always asking for value on edit (#2671)\n\n### Storage & Data\n\n- **Evaluator Parsing**: Fixed evaluator not erroring on parsing failures (#2918)\n- **Redis Configuration**: Added support for username parameter in Redis configuration (#2953)\n\n---\n\n## Upgrade Guide\n\n### Step 1: Review Deprecations\n\nBefore upgrading, identify which deprecated APIs your applications use:\n- Check if you're calling `Flipt.Evaluate()` or `Flipt.BatchEvaluate()`\n- Verify if your list requests use the `offset` parameter\n- Check if rules/rollouts reference single `segment_key` fields\n\n### Step 2: Update Evaluation Calls\n\n**If using the legacy Evaluate method:**\n\n```protobuf\n// OLD: Using deprecated unified evaluation\nEvaluationResponse response = client.Evaluate(EvaluationRequest{\n  flag_key: \"my_flag\",\n  entity_id: \"user123\"\n});\n\n// NEW: Use type-specific endpoints\nBooleanEvaluationResponse boolResponse = client.Boolean(EvaluationRequest{\n  namespace_key: \"default\",\n  flag_key: \"my_flag\",\n  entity_id: \"user123\"\n});\n\n// Or for variants:\nVariantEvaluationResponse variantResponse = client.Variant(EvaluationRequest{\n  namespace_key: \"default\",\n  flag_key: \"my_flag\",\n  entity_id: \"user123\"\n});\n```\n\n### Step 3: Migrate Pagination\n\n**If using offset-based pagination:**\n\n```protobuf\n// OLD: Offset-based\nListFlagRequest{\n  namespace_key: \"default\",\n  limit: 50,\n  offset: 100  // Skip first 100 items\n}\n\n// NEW: Cursor-based\nListFlagRequest{\n  namespace_key: \"default\",\n  limit: 50,\n  page_token: \"eyJvZmZzZXQiOjEwMH0=\" // Flipt Release Notes\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\n> These changes require action from users upgrading.\n\n### API Evaluation Endpoints - Migrating from Legacy Evaluate Methods\n\nThe legacy `Flipt.Evaluate` and `Flipt.BatchEvaluate` RPC methods are **deprecated** and will be removed in a future release.\n\n**Migration Path:**\n- **For Boolean Flags**: Use the dedicated `EvaluationService.Boolean(EvaluationRequest)` endpoint instead\n- **For Variant Flags**: Use the dedicated `EvaluationService.Variant(EvaluationRequest)` endpoint instead\n- **For Batch Operations**: Use `EvaluationService.Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest)` for batched evaluations\n\nThe new evaluation API provides structured response types (`BooleanEvaluationResponse`, `VariantEvaluationResponse`, and `ErrorEvaluationResponse`) that offer better type safety and clearer semantics compared to the legacy single-response structure.\n\n**Example:**\n```protobuf\n// Old API (deprecated)\nrpc Evaluate(EvaluationRequest) returns (EvaluationResponse)\n\n// New API\nrpc Boolean(EvaluationRequest) returns (BooleanEvaluationResponse)\nrpc Variant(EvaluationRequest) returns (VariantEvaluationResponse)\n```\n\n### Pagination API Change - Offset to Cursor-Based Pagination\n\nThe `offset` parameter is **deprecated** in list request messages:\n- `ListNamespaceRequest`\n- `ListFlagRequest`\n- `ListSegmentRequest`\n- `ListRuleRequest`\n\n**Migration Path:**\nReplace all `offset`-based pagination with the `page_token` parameter:\n- Use `page_token` returned in the `next_page_token` field of list responses for pagination\n- Remove reliance on `offset` parameter\n- If you need to restart pagination, don't provide `page_token` (equivalent to offset=0)\n\n**Example:**\n```protobuf\n// Before (deprecated)\nmessage ListFlagRequest {\n  int32 limit = 1;\n  int32 offset = 2;  // [deprecated]\n}\n\n// After\nmessage ListFlagRequest {\n  int32 limit = 1;\n  int32 offset = 2;     // [deprecated = true]\n  string page_token = 3; // Use this instead\n}\n```\n\n### Single Segment to Multi-Segment Rules\n\nThe `segment_key` field is **deprecated** in favor of the new `segment_keys` array and `segment_operator` field for rules and rollouts.\n\n**Migration Path:**\n- Rules: Update to use `segment_keys` (array) and `segment_operator` (OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR or AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR) instead of single `segment_key`\n- Rollouts: Update to use `RolloutSegment.segment_keys` and `segment_operator` instead of `segment_key`\n- The old fields will continue to work but may be removed in a future release\n\n**Example:**\n```protobuf\n// Before (deprecated)\nmessage CreateRuleRequest {\n  string flag_key = 1;\n  string segment_key = 2;  // [deprecated = true]\n}\n\n// After - Support multiple segments with operators\nmessage CreateRuleRequest {\n  string flag_key = 1;\n  string segment_key = 2;              // [deprecated = true]\n  repeated string segment_keys = 5;    // Use this\n  SegmentOperator segment_operator = 6; // AND or OR\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### Enhanced Evaluation API with Type-Specific Endpoints\n\n**Component: gRPC Evaluation Service (`flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService`)**\n\nNew dedicated evaluation endpoints for better API clarity and type safety:\n- `Boolean(EvaluationRequest)` → `BooleanEvaluationResponse` - For boolean flag evaluation\n- `Variant(EvaluationRequest)` → `VariantEvaluationResponse` - For variant flag evaluation\n- `Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest)` → `BatchEvaluationResponse` - For batched evaluations\n\nResponse types now distinguish between success and error cases with `EvaluationResponseType` enum (VARIANT_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE, BOOLEAN_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE, ERROR_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE).\n\n### Multiple Segment Support in Rules and Rollouts\n\n**Component: Rules and Rollouts API**\n\nRules and rollouts can now reference multiple segments with AND/OR logic:\n- `SegmentOperator` enum: OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR (default) or AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR\n- Rules support `repeated string segment_keys` with `SegmentOperator`\n- Rollouts support `RolloutSegment.segment_keys` with `segment_operator`\n\nThis enables complex targeting scenarios such as:\n- Rule matches if entity is in \"beta_users\" AND \"premium_subscribers\"\n- Rollout targets all users EXCEPT those matching specific segments\n\n### Boolean Flag Type and Evaluation\n\n**Component: Core Flags API**\n\nNew FlagType enum value: `BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE` (in addition to existing VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE)\n\nBoolean flags have dedicated evaluation endpoints:\n- `EvaluationService.Boolean()` - Returns `BooleanEvaluationResponse` with enabled/disabled state\n- Boolean rollouts: `RolloutThreshold` type supports percentage-based rollouts with boolean values\n- Boolean rules: Can distribute boolean true/false values through distributions\n\n**API Example:**\n```protobuf\nmessage CreateFlagRequest {\n  string key = 1;\n  string name = 2;\n  FlagType type = 6; // VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE or BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE\n}\n```\n\n### Advanced Constraint Operators\n\n**Component: Constraints API**\n\nNew constraint operators for segment targeting:\n- `IS ONE OF` - Value matches one of the provided values\n- `IS NOT ONE OF` - Value does not match any of the provided values\n\nThese work with existing comparison types: STRING_COMPARISON_TYPE, NUMBER_COMPARISON_TYPE, BOOLEAN_COMPARISON_TYPE, DATETIME_COMPARISON_TYPE, ENTITY_ID_COMPARISON_TYPE.\n\n### Entity ID Constraint Type\n\n**Component: Constraints API**\n\nNew `ENTITY_ID_COMPARISON_TYPE` for constraint evaluation enables comparing entity IDs directly in segment constraints, useful for allow-listing or block-listing specific users/entities.\n\n### Namespaced Authentication Tokens\n\n**Component: Auth API (`flipt.auth.AuthenticationMethodTokenService`)**\n\nAuthentication tokens can now be scoped to specific namespaces:\n- `CreateTokenRequest` includes optional `namespace_key` field\n- Namespaced tokens can only access resources within their designated namespace\n- Improves multi-tenant security and isolation\n\n**API Example:**\n```protobuf\nmessage CreateTokenRequest {\n  string name = 1;\n  string description = 2;\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp expires_at = 3;\n  string namespace_key = 4; // Optional: scope to namespace\n}\n```\n\n### GitHub Authentication with Team Membership\n\n**Component: Auth API (`flipt.auth.AuthenticationMethodGithubService`)**\n\nGitHub authentication now supports team membership verification:\n- Check if authenticated user belongs to specific GitHub organization teams\n- Adds `AuthenticationMethodGithubService` with OAuth flow support\n- Complements existing GitHub organization membership checks\n\n### JWT Authentication Method\n\n**Component: Auth API**\n\nNew JWT authentication method available:\n- `Method.METHOD_JWT` enum value\n- Enables JWT token validation for API authentication\n- Supports custom JWT claims and validation rules\n\n### Multi-Storage Backend Support\n\n**Component: Storage Layer**\n\nEnhanced support for multiple storage backends:\n- **S3 Filesystem Backend**: S3 bucket support with prefix filtering for organized data structures\n- **Google Cloud Storage (GCS)**: Full GCS integration for filesystem-based flag storage\n- **Azure Blob Storage**: Azure integration for filesystem operations\n- **OCI (Object Container Interface)**: OCI storage with AWS ECR integration and configurable manifest versions\n- **LibSQL/Turso**: SQLite-compatible database support\n\nEach backend integrates with the filesystem abstraction layer supporting both SQL and non-SQL deployments.\n\n### Directory Scope for Git Backend\n\n**Component: Storage/Git Backend (`fs/git`)**\n\nNew configuration support for Git-based flag storage:\n- `directory_scope` parameter for limiting Git operations to a specific directory\n- Useful for monorepos or multi-service Git repositories\n- Restricts flag definitions to a designated directory subtree\n\n### Working Directory Support for Flipt Validate\n\n**Component: CLI (flipt validate)**\n\n`flipt validate` command now accepts a working directory parameter:\n- Allows validation to run in a specific directory context\n- Useful in CI/CD pipelines with multiple flag definitions\n- Validates flag YAML/CUE schemas in the specified directory\n\n### Rollout Descriptions\n\n**Component: Rollouts API**\n\nRollouts can now include descriptions:\n- `Rollout.description` field for documenting rollout purpose and logic\n- Included in rollout cards in the UI\n- Helps teams understand complex rollout strategies\n\n### Analytics with Clickhouse Support\n\n**Component: Analytics API (`flipt.analytics.AnalyticsService`)**\n\nNew analytics backend and API:\n- `AnalyticsService.GetFlagEvaluationsCount()` - Retrieves evaluation count metrics\n- Clickhouse database integration for time-series analytics\n- Supports time range queries (from/to parameters)\n- Returns timestamps and evaluation values for visualization\n\n**API Example:**\n```protobuf\nrpc GetFlagEvaluationsCount(GetFlagEvaluationsCountRequest)\n    returns (GetFlagEvaluationsCountResponse)\n\nmessage GetFlagEvaluationsCountRequest {\n  string namespace_key = 1;\n  string flag_key = 2;\n  string from = 3;  // Timestamp\n  string to = 4;    // Timestamp\n}\n```\n\n### Kubernetes Authentication Provider (SDK)\n\n**Component: SDK/Go Auth**\n\nNew Kubernetes service account authentication provider for SDK:\n- `AuthenticationMethodKubernetesService.VerifyServiceAccount()`\n- Enables pod-to-pod authentication using Kubernetes service account tokens\n- Useful for Kubernetes-native deployments\n\n### Redis Cache Improvements\n\n**Component: Storage/Cache**\n\nEnhanced Redis cache configuration:\n- Support for Redis username in authentication (in addition to password)\n- Improved connection handling\n- Only stores authentication hashes in cache (not full credentials)\n\n---\n\n## Deprecations\n\n### Legacy Evaluate RPC Methods\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.40.0 (or earlier)\n- **What**: `Flipt.Evaluate()` and `Flipt.BatchEvaluate()` RPC methods\n- **Replacement**: Use `EvaluationService.Boolean()`, `EvaluationService.Variant()`, or `EvaluationService.Batch()`\n- **Timeline**: Will be removed in a future major version\n\n### Offset-Based Pagination\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.13.0\n- **What**: `offset` field in list requests (ListFlagRequest, ListSegmentRequest, ListRuleRequest, ListNamespaceRequest)\n- **Replacement**: Use `page_token` for cursor-based pagination\n- **Timeline**: ~1 year from deprecation date (June 2024)\n\n### Single Segment Fields\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.31.0+\n- **What**: `segment_key` field in `CreateRuleRequest`, `UpdateRuleRequest`, `RolloutSegment.segment_key`\n- **Replacement**: Use `segment_keys` (array) with `segment_operator` for AND/OR logic\n- **Timeline**: ~1 year from deprecation date\n\n### Jaeger Tracing Exporter\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.36.0\n- **What**: Jaeger tracing exporter support\n- **Replacement**: Use OpenTelemetry Protocol (OTLP) with official Jaeger OTLP receiver\n- **Reason**: OpenTelemetry dropped official Jaeger exporter support in July 2023\n- **Timeline**: Already removed in recent versions\n\n### Authentication Metadata Exclusion Configuration\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.37.0\n- **What**: `authentication.exclude.metadata` configuration option\n- **Replacement**: Configure metadata handling directly in auth method settings\n- **Timeline**: ~6 months from deprecation date (May 2024)\n\n---\n\n## Bug Fixes\n\n### Critical Fixes\n\n- **isnotoneof Operator Logic**: Fixed operator using incorrect logic for segment constraint evaluation (#2912)\n- **Segment Constraints in Different Namespaces**: Resolved issue where segment constraints with the same key in different namespaces caused evaluation errors (#2920)\n- **Batch Evaluation exclude_not_found**: Fixed batched evaluation to properly exclude not-found responses when requested\n\n### Authentication & Security\n\n- **Auth Cache Security**: Only store authentication hash in cache, not full credentials (#2974)\n- **Database Connection Optimization**: Skip establishing database connection in auth when unnecessary (#2973)\n- **Email Matching on OIDC**: Only enforce email matches on OIDC method tokens, not other auth methods (#1934)\n\n### Configuration & Validation\n\n- **Trace Log Level Schema**: Fixed invalid trace log level schema validation\n- **Rollout Segment JSON Schema**: Corrected jsonschema validation for key|keys in rollout segment definitions (#2947)\n- **Page Token Validation**: value on edit (#2671)\n\n### Storage & Data\n\n- **Evaluator Parsing**: Fixed evaluator not erroring on parsing failures (#2918)\n- **Redis Configuration**: Added support for username parameter in Redis configuration (#2953)\n\n---\n\n## Upgrade Guide\n\n### Step 1: Review Deprecations\n\nBefore upgrading, identify which deprecated APIs your applications use:\n- Check if you're calling
